<h3 class="section-title">Other Ways to Get Involved</h3>
<div class="container">
<div class="row">
<div class="col-sm-3 ">
<div class="project">
<a href="https://www.headcount.org/headcount-initiatives/?project=participation-row" class="thumbnail-link show-title-on" style="background-image: url('https://www.headcount.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/ParticipationRow-1200-150x150.jpg'); background-size: cover;">
<h3>Participation Row</h3>
</a>
<p>HeadCount organizes &#8220;Participation Row&#8221; social-action villages and charity auctions at major live music events, with help from sponsors Qello and Clean Energy Advisors.</p>
<a class="read-more" href="https://www.headcount.org/headcount-initiatives/?project=participation-row">Get Started</a>
</div>
<div class="ribbon ribbon-white left"></div>
</div>
<div class="col-sm-3 offset">
<div class="project">
<a href="https://www.headcount.org/headcount-initiatives/?project=capitol-community-auctions" class="thumbnail-link show-title-on" style="background-image: url('https://www.headcount.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Capitol-Theatre-IMG-1-150x150.jpg'); background-size: cover;">
<h3>Capitol Community</h3>
</a>
<p>The Capitol Community Fund is a HeadCount project that sends area teachers to the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame and Museum to receive curriculum training on how to bring music history into classrooms, emphasizing the interplay between popular music and activism.</p>
<a class="read-more" href="https://www.headcount.org/headcount-initiatives/?project=capitol-community-auctions">Check It Out</a>
</div>
<div class="ribbon ribbon-white right"></div>
</div>
<div class="col-sm-3 ">
<div class="project">
<a href="https://www.headcount.org/headcount-initiatives/?project=soundoff" class="thumbnail-link">
<img src="https://www.headcount.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/SoundOff.png" alt="#SoundOff">
</a>
<p>Tweet directly @ Congress. Pick a topic, enter your zip, and type your message. #SoundOff sends the message to your House Rep or Senators on the issues that matter to you.</p>
<a class="read-more" href="https://www.headcount.org/headcount-initiatives/?project=soundoff">Learn More</a>
</div>
<div class="ribbon ribbon-white left"></div>
</div>
<div class="col-sm-3 offset">
<a href="https://www.headcount.org/headcount-initiatives" id="more-projects">
<i class="fa fa-arrow-circle-right"></i>
More Headcount Initiatives & Projects
</a>
<div class="ribbon ribbon-red right"></div>
</div>

<h3 class="page-title"><a href="https://www.headcount.org/think-youre-young-register/" rel="bookmark">Think You&#8217;re Too Young to Register?</a></h3>
<div class="entry-summary">
<p>Think you’re not old enough to register to vote? If you&#8217;re 17 and will be 18 by Election Day, chances are you can. Check out our chart below that details when you are eligible to register or preregister in your state, and when you can start voting! &nbsp; Click Here to Register To Vote Alaska: You&#8230;</p>

Before the show and during setbreak, the entire band met with the group and shared some inspirational words. The group included many of the students who&#8230;</p>

<script>
	$('a').each(function() {
   var a = new RegExp('/' + window.location.host + '/');
   if(!a.test(this.href)) {
       $(this).click(function(event) {
           event.preventDefault();
           event.stopPropagation();
           window.open(this.href, '_blank');
       });
   }});
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
	// The function actually applying the offset
	function offsetAnchor() {
	    if(location.hash.length !== 0) {
	        window.scrollTo(window.scrollX, window.scrollY - 200);
	    }
	}

	// This will capture hash changes while on the page
	window.addEventListener("hashchange", offsetAnchor);

	// This is here so that when you enter the page with a hash,
	// it can provide the offset in that case too. Having a timeout
	// seems necessary to allow the browser to jump to the anchor first.
	window.setTimeout(offsetAnchor, 1); // The delay of 1 is arbitrary and may not always work right (although it did in my testing).
</script>
